**Devices:** Existential pattern: Place + verb + 着/了 + numeral + measure word + noun (靠窗户摆着两张书桌 / 柜子里挂着一些衣服 / 门右边放着两个书架); Spatial anchors chained one to the next: 靠窗户→旁边→床上→床旁边→门右边; Measure-word precision: 张 (desk), 把 (chair), 个 (wardrobe/bookshelf); 是 vs 有 to signal a single item vs. multiple items at a location

张天明宿舍的房间不太大，住两个人。他的同屋已经来了。房间里家具不多，靠窗户摆着两张书桌，每张桌子的前边有一把椅子。书桌的旁边是床，床上有被子和毯子。床旁边有两个衣柜，柜子里挂着一些衣服。门右边放着两个书架，书架还是空的。

---

### 在饭馆儿（点菜叙事开头）  ·  _narrative lead-in to a dialogue_

*A narrative setup: on a free weekend Zhang Tianming WeChats Ke Lin about getting Chinese food; Ke Lin drives over, and they discover a fourth person, exchange student Lin Xuemei, before arriving at the restaurant.*

**Why study:** A model for the narrative 'frame' that sets up a scene before dialogue. It shows topic-fronting of known information and tight action sequencing with time phrases.

**Devices:** Topic-comment opening with given information fronted: 今天是周末，功课也做完了; 就 to mark the natural next action (发微信 / 让…等着); Momentary 一 + verb: 上车一看 ('took one look and saw…'); Time-stamped sequencing: 半个钟头以后…几分钟以后…; Reported speech with 说/问/介绍说 to compress dialogue into narration

今天是周末，功课也做完了，张天明就给柯林发微信，说他和他的女朋友丽莎想吃中国饭，问他想不想去。柯林说正好他也想吃中国饭，就让张天明和丽莎在宿舍门口等着，他开车来接他们。半个钟头以后，柯林的汽车到了。张天明和丽莎上车一看，车里还有一个女孩儿，柯林介绍说，她是从中国来的留学生，叫林雪梅。几分钟以后，他们四个人到了那家中国饭馆儿。

---

### 住校外的三个理由（柯林的回答）  ·  _argumentative dialogue turn_

*Ke Lin explains why he lives off campus: some prefer dorms for convenience and safety, others off campus for cheaper rent; he himself lives off campus to save money and for freedom, adding that on-campus living isn't necessarily convenient.*

**Why study:** A textbook demonstration of stacking connectives to deliver an organized, persuasive answer rather than a flat list. The same content is also shown reorganized with 第一/第二/第三, illustrating two equivalent structuring strategies.

**Devices:** Contrast framing: 有的人…，有的人…; Reason chain: 因为 + 除了…以外，还 + 再说; Polite hedge 不见得 to soften a counter-claim; Paired-adjective 又方便又安全; Alternative enumeration via 第一…，第二…，第三… (shown as a variant)

有的人喜欢住在学校宿舍，觉得又方便又安全，有的人喜欢住在校外，因为校外的房子比较便宜。我住在校外，除了想省点儿钱以外，还因为住在校外自由。再说，住在校内也不见得很方便。

---

### 在中国饭馆儿吃饭 (Eating at a Chinese Restaurant)  ·  _Narrative description / cohesion model_

*A short third-person account of four friends ordering at a Chinese restaurant: which dishes the place does well, what they ordered, and the special requests Ke Lin made to the waiter (lighter seasoning, less salt, less oil, no MSG).*

**Why study:** The textbook explicitly presents this as a 'Keep It Flowing' model for cohesion. It shows how to turn a list of facts (good dishes -> dishes ordered -> special requests) into a smoothly connected paragraph rather than disjointed sentences. Excellent template for any 'describe a dining experience' or recommendation paragraph.

**Devices:** Definite reference 那个/那儿 replaces the indefinite first mention 一家饭馆儿 (introduce-then-refer-back); Causal connective 所以 links the dishes' merits to the ordering decision; Emphasis marker 特别是 singles out the standout dish (清蒸鱼); Additive adverbs 也 / 还 stack parallel positives (鱼也…，那儿还有…); Descriptive 又…又… (又嫩又香) compresses two qualities into one phrase; Time/place words (周末, 那儿) act as connective anchors

周末，张天明、丽莎、柯林和柯林的女朋友林雪梅一起在一家中国饭馆儿吃饭。那个饭馆儿鸡做得不错，鱼也做得很好，特别是清蒸鱼，味道好极了。那儿的芥蓝牛肉也挺好，又嫩又香，菠菜豆腐汤做得也很好，那儿还有有机的小白菜。所以他们点了一个清蒸鱼，一个芥蓝牛肉，一个菠菜豆腐汤和一个小白菜。柯林告诉服务员，菜要清淡一点儿，别太咸，少放油，别放味精。他们的菜很快就来了。

---

### 张天明和柯林买衣服的标准 (Zhang Tianming's and Ke Lin's Clothes-Buying Criteria)  ·  _Expository / comparison-contrast model_

*Contrasts two characters' shopping philosophies: Zhang Tianming insists only on brand names (believing they are higher quality), while Ke Lin ranks comfort, quality, and price over brand and fashion, arguing one dresses for oneself, not for others. Ends with Zhang catching Ke Lin wearing a brand-name item and Ke Lin's distinction (he never said he wouldn't wear brands, only that he wouldn't insist on buying them).*

**Why study:** A clean model for structured comparison of two viewpoints and for listing prioritized criteria with 第一…第二…第三…. Shows how to state a position, give a reason, then handle a counterpoint/apparent contradiction logically.

**Devices:** Ordinal enumeration 第一…第二…第三… to rank criteria; Pronoun 他 keeps the subject unchanged across sentences without repeating the name; Conjunctions 要不然 (otherwise), 因为 (cause), 但是 (contrast) chain the logic; Adverb 就 ties consequence to condition (要不然就不买 / 就问柯林); Parallel negation 不在乎…，也不在乎… for balanced emphasis; 是为了…不是为了… frames purpose vs. non-purpose neatly; Resolving an apparent contradiction by drawing a fine distinction (买 vs. 穿)

张天明买衣服一定要买名牌的，要不然就不买，因为他觉得名牌的衣服质量好。柯林觉得买衣服只考虑便宜当然不好，但是不一定非买名牌的不可。他买衣服的标准，第一看穿着舒服不舒服，第二看质量好不好，第三看价钱合适不合适。他不在乎是什么牌子的，也不在乎样子时髦不时髦。他认为穿衣服是为了自己，不是为了给别人看。张天明看见柯林穿了一件名牌衣服，就问柯林为什么穿名牌的衣服？柯林说，他说过不一定非买名牌的不可，但是没说过不穿名牌呀。

---

### 下个学期选什么课？ (Which Classes to Take Next Semester?)  ·  _Narrative summary / cohesion model_

*A condensed retelling of a longer dialogue: Zhang Tianming's current four courses, his wish for a lighter next semester, his chat with Li Zhe leading him to also pick economics and computing, and the tension over majors (he likes literature but his mother insists on finance; Li Zhe notes many classmates have more freedom).*

**Why study:** Demonstrates how to compress a multi-turn dialogue into a tight third-person summary—a key academic writing skill. Models sequencing with time words and reporting both hearsay and speech without quoting verbatim.

**Devices:** Pronouns 他/他们 replace names once the subject is established; redundant subject omitted (shown as [他]); Time/sequence words 现在, 这一天下午, 然后 advance the narrative; Reporting verbs 听说 (hearsay) and …说 (reported speech) fold dialogue into narration; Contrast/cause conjunctions 可是, 因为 connect clauses; 非…不可 dramatizes the mother's insistence inside reported speech

张天明这个学期选了四门课：世界历史、电脑、政治学和中文。他觉得这几门课都很有意思，也学到了不少东西。现在得选下学期的课了，他希望下个学期能轻松点儿。这一天下午，他跟李哲聊选课的事。听说李哲要选经济和电脑课，他很高兴，[他]也决定选这两门课。然后他们又聊选专业的事。张天明说他喜欢文学，可是他妈妈非叫他学他不喜欢的金融不可。李哲说他们班很多同学选专业很自由，因为他们的父母不太管孩子选什么专业。

---

### 买东西 (Shopping) — Lesson 4 dialogue  ·  _Dialogue_

*Four friends go to a mall: Zhang shops for a tracksuit while the others buy daily necessities. The dialogue debates buying name-brand vs. cheap clothing, lays out criteria for choosing clothes, and ends at checkout (cash vs. card, tax added to the total).*

**Why study:** Practical register for shopping, expressing discounts (打八折), describing fit (样子/大小/长短都合适), tactful disagreement, and a checkout exchange. Useful sentence frames for everyday transactional Chinese.

**Devices:** 无论…都… to dismiss every option at once (style and color both no good); …什么的 to cap a list of examples; Partial-agreement frame 便宜是便宜，可是… for tactful pushback; Criteria listing 第一…第二…第三…; Transactional set phrases: 打八折, 付现金/刷卡, 加上税一共是…

张天明从家里来的时候，妈妈给他买了一些衣服，像T恤衫、毛衣、牛仔裤什么的，可是他觉得无论是样子还是颜色都不太好。今天是星期日，正好林雪梅和丽莎也需要买卫生纸、牙膏、毛巾、洗衣粉这些日用品，柯林就带他们来到附近一家最大的购物中心。
—你要买什么衣服？
—我想买一套运动服。
—这边儿就是。你看看这一套，样子、大小、长短都合适，而且打八折。
—颜色也不错。多少钱？是什么牌子的？
—价钱不贵。这个牌子没听说过。不过，是纯棉的。
—牌子不好不行，我想买名牌的。
…（讨论名牌 vs. 便宜、质量）…
—我买衣服的标准，第一是看穿着舒服不舒服，第二是质量好不好，第三是价钱合适不合适。是什么牌子的，样子时髦不时髦，我都不在乎。因为穿衣服是为了自己，不是为了给别人看。
…（付钱）…
—先生，付现金，还是用信用卡？
—我刷卡。
—先生，加上税一共是一百八十六块四。

---

### 丽莎的心事 (Lisa's Worry) — Lesson 6 opening narrative  ·  _Narrative (relationship/dating)_

*A third-person narrative plus dialogue: Lisa has been troubled because she quarreled with her boyfriend Zhang Tianming over his forgetfulness (he forgot a concert date). Lin Xuemei reassures her that being scatterbrained is different from not caring, noting her own boyfriend Ke Lin is similarly forgetful.*

**Why study:** Rich source of personality/feeling vocabulary and high-frequency colloquial idioms for describing forgetful, easygoing people and emotional states. Models how narration and reported dialogue interleave in a story.

**Devices:** 一…就… (一有球赛就…，一有演唱会就…) for habitual immediate reactions; 非…不可 for compulsive behavior (他就非看不可); 想来想去 / 想不出 reduplication + potential complement to show pondering; Vivid set idioms: 忘得一干二净, 丢三落四, 忘这忘那; 原来 to mark a realization; 到底 to press for the real story

丽莎这几天好像有什么心事。昨天林雪梅问了她好几次，她才说她跟张天明吵架了。…天明人很好，很开朗，学习也不错。在兴趣上她跟天明不太一样，天明是个球迷，电视里一有球赛，他就非看不可，丽莎是个歌迷，一有演唱会就去听。…林雪梅想来想去，想不出他们到底发生了什么事儿。…两个星期前我跟他约好去看一个演唱会，没想到他那天晚上一直玩儿电脑，把演唱会的事儿忘得一干二净。…他不停地给我道歉，说对不起，态度特别好。这让我觉得他心里还是有我。…实际上，柯林跟天明差不多，常常忘这忘那、丢三落四的。

---

### 张天明太马虎了  ·  _Descriptive narrative (character sketch)_

*A short profile of Zhang Tianming: likeable, cheerful, a sports fan, but extremely careless. Two anecdotes prove the point—he forgot a concert date entirely, and he went to the wrong movie theater—ending with an exclamatory verdict.*

**Why study:** A textbook 'Keep It Flowing' model showing how to build a coherent paragraph around a single trait (马虎) using concrete examples rather than mere adjectives. Demonstrates topic-sentence + supporting-evidence + closing structure.

**Devices:** Topic sentence stating the trait (太马虎了), then proving it with two parallel anecdotes; Time phrases as connectors: 两个星期前 / 那天晚上 / 上个星期六 / 八点的电影; Pronoun 他 substituting for 张天明 to avoid repetition; 一…就 (一有球赛就非看不可) and 才 (等到八点一刻…才知道) as cohesive adverbs; Complement of result 忘得一干二净 to intensify the description; Exclamatory closing (这个天明，真马虎！) echoing the opening for a frame

张天明人很好，很开朗，学习也不错。他是个球迷，电视里一有球赛，就非看不可。可是他非常马虎。两个星期前丽莎跟他约好去看一个演唱会，那天晚上他一直玩儿电脑，把演唱会的事儿忘得一干二净。上个星期六丽莎让他一起去看电影，他很高兴地答应了。八点的电影，丽莎等到八点一刻他还没到，给他打手机，才知道他跑到另一家电影院去了。这个天明，真马虎！

---

### 张天明是个电脑迷  ·  _Descriptive narrative (character sketch)_

*A compact portrait of Zhang Tianming as a computer addict: his daily online activities, his reliance on the Internet for research, and his self-justification that in the Internet age one naturally cannot do without a computer.*

**Why study:** A model for the 'define-a-type-then-illustrate' paragraph. Shows how to list activities economically with a serial 顿号 structure and how to close with the subject's own voice (他说…) to round off a description.

**Devices:** Opening label sentence (X 是个…迷) that the rest of the paragraph unpacks; Serial listing with 顿号: 看新闻、查资料、玩儿游戏; Time-frequency adverbs as connectors: 每天 / 有时候 / 的时候 / 常常; 一…就 (一上网就忘了时间) showing habitual cause-effect; Reported judgment (别人说…) vs. the subject's rebuttal (他说…) for a balanced close; 一会儿都离不开 emphatic negation for vividness

张天明是个电脑迷。每天在网上看新闻、查资料、玩儿游戏，有时候还在自己的网站上写博客，一会儿都离不开电脑，常常一上网，就忘了时间。他写文章的时候，喜欢上网查资料，觉得网上很多资料很可靠很有用。别人说他玩儿电脑上瘾了。他说现在是网络时代，当然离不开电脑。

---

### 张天明想打工 (Lesson 8 opening)  ·  _Expository narrative introduction_

*Sets up the part-time-work theme: the parents save for education from birth and, despite decent income, feel financial pressure supporting two children in college; Tianming, feeling grown-up, goes online to look for a suitable job to ease their burden, just as Lisa and Xuemei walk in.*

**Why study:** A model of how to open an essay or story by establishing background (cause), motivation, and an action, then handing off to dialogue. Good template for the 'situation → reasoning → decision' setup move.

**Devices:** 虽然…但是… concessive frame to acknowledge income yet assert pressure; 所以 / 应该…来… chaining cause to intended action (找工作挣钱来减轻负担); 一…就 (一生下来就开始存) for immediacy; Scene-handoff sentence (这时候…走了进来) to transition from narration into dialogue

张天明的父母希望孩子们能受到良好的教育，所以孩子一生下来就开始给他们存教育费。虽然张天明父母的收入不少，但是供天明和姐姐上大学，经济上还是有些压力。张天明觉得自己已经是大人了，应该找工作挣钱来减轻父母的负担，所以就上网看看有没有适合自己的工作。这时候丽莎和雪梅走了进来。

---

### 电脑和网络 (Lesson 7 dialogue)  ·  _Conversational dialogue_

*Friends confront Tianming for being late again because he lost track of time downloading software and browsing online. The chat ranges over the reliability of online vs. print sources, the convenience of the Internet for everyday needs, an apology exchange, and a pivot to change the subject.*

**Why study:** A model of natural intermediate dialogue: apologizing, debating a point, and tactfully closing an awkward exchange. Useful template for register-appropriate spoken connectors and reduplicated softeners.

**Devices:** 结果 to mark an unintended outcome (结果忘了时间); Reduplicated apology/pacifier: 对不起，对不起 / 好了，好了; Rhetorical question to scold gently: 你说我该不该生气？; 又…又… parallelism for praise: 网络世界又大又方便; Catch-all enumeration 衣食住行，什么都查得到; Topic-change pivot phrase: 好了，好了，不说这些了

对不起，对不起，我在网上下载了一个软件，又查了一点儿东西，结果忘了时间了。——查什么？——我要写一篇文章，查一些资料。——查资料？我们的教授不让我们用网上的东西，一定要用书或者杂志。他说网上的垃圾太多了。——你的教授太落伍了，网上有很多资料很可靠很有用啊。网络世界又大又方便，你可以叫外卖、购物，你可以租房子、买车，衣食住行，什么都查得到。——哎，丽莎，你还在生我的气吗？——你说我该不该生气？你每次都迟到，老是害得大家等你。——对不起，对不起，是我不好。下次不敢了。——好了，好了，不说这些了，我们到底去哪家卡拉OK啊？

---

### 中国地理  ·  _expository paragraph / geography description_

*A concise expository paragraph describing China's geography: the high plateau in the west contrasting with eastern plains and sea; eastward river flow driven by terrain; concentration of population and major cities along the coast due to favorable natural conditions; sparse population in the mountainous southwest and desert northwest.*

**Why study:** The textbook presents this explicitly as a 'Keep It Flowing' model, highlighting its cohesive devices. It demonstrates how to use conjunctions, anaphoric place pronouns, causal constructions, and the topic marker 呢 to chain short sentences into fluent expository prose. The register is clean, semi-formal, and directly transferable to academic writing, geography presentations, or any topic requiring logical spatial/causal sequencing.

**Devices:** 而 as contrastive conjunction between parallel clauses (西边是高原…而东边是平原和大海); 那儿 as anaphoric place pronoun linking back to the previously mentioned location (西边是高原，那儿有…); 因为…所以… explicit cause-effect frame making the logical chain transparent; 也 as additive connective within a clause (大城市也都靠海); Sentence-initial 而 to pivot to a contrasting new topic (而中国的西南，高山、高原多); X呢 topic marker introducing a parallel comparison (西北呢，沙漠多); 大多 as formal adverb for 'mostly / for the most part' (大多是从西往东流); Parallel repetition of 所以 to build layered causal structure

中国的面积很大。西边是高原，那儿有世界上最高的山，而东边是平原和大海，所以中国的河流，大多是从西往东流。因为东部和南部自然条件比较好，所以人口主要在这些地方，大城市也都靠海或者离海不远。而中国的西南，高山、高原多，西北呢，沙漠多，自然条件不太好，所以人口比较少。

---
